    <script type="text/javascript">
     function ham_news_behavior(){
	let HAM = document.querySelector('.hamburger_newsletter_container'),
HAMFORM=HAM.querySelector('form');

HAMFORM.addEventListener("submit", function(e){
    e.preventDefault();
    
    var S = document.createElement('script');
    let groups = {};
    HAM.querySelectorAll("#groups input").forEach(function(I) {
        if(I.checked) {
            groups[I.getAttribute("name")] = true;
        }
    });

    var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
    xhr.open('POST', 'https://www.protocol.com/core/mail_lists/mailchimp/access/');
    xhr.setRequestHeader('Content-Type', 'application/json');
    xhr.onload = function() {
        if (xhr.status === 200) {
            var response = JSON.parse(xhr.responseText);
            let resp = HAM.querySelector('#MC_resp');
            //resetBAR(resp);

            if (response.created !== true) {
              resp.classList.add('bad');
              resp.innerHTML = 'Temporary error. Please try again later.';
            } else {
              resp.classList.add('good');
              email.value = '';
              resp.innerHTML = 'Thank you for subscribing!';
            }
        } else if (xhr.status === 400) {
            var response = JSON.parse(xhr.responseText);
            let resp = HAM.querySelector('#MC_resp');
            //resetBAR(resp);
            resp.innerHTML = response.error;
            resp.classList.add('bad');
        }
    };
    xhr.send(JSON.stringify({
        email: HAM.querySelector('#MC_email').value,
        group_ids: groups,
        list_id: 'cd425f6479'
    }));
});
}
  
(function(){

  if (window.innerWidth < 768){
    let menu_global=document.querySelector('.rebelbar');
      if(menu_global){
        menu_global.querySelector('.site-share-placeholder').insertAdjacentElement('afterend',document.querySelector('.hamburger_newsletter_container').cloneNode(true));
        document.querySelectorAll('.hamburger_newsletter_container')[1].remove(); 
        ham_news_behavior();
      }
  }else{
    var navbarItems = document.querySelectorAll('.navbar-sections__item');

    navbarItems.forEach(function(el) {
      var dropdown = el.querySelector('.navbar-sections__dropdown')
      if(dropdown) {
        el.onmouseover = function() {
          el.classList.add('active')
          if (typeof checkRunnerLazyLoadedItems === "function") {
            checkRunnerLazyLoadedItems();
          }
        }
        el.onmouseout = function() {
          el.classList.remove('active')
        }
      }
    });
    
    let menu_global=document.querySelector('.menu-global');
    if(menu_global){
      menu_global.insertAdjacentElement('afterbegin',document.querySelector('.site-links').cloneNode(true));
      menu_global.querySelector('.site-links').insertAdjacentElement('afterend',document.querySelector('.site-share-placeholder').cloneNode(true));
      menu_global.querySelector('.site-share-placeholder').insertAdjacentElement('afterend',document.querySelector('.hamburger_newsletter_container').cloneNode(true));
      document.querySelectorAll('.hamburger_newsletter_container')[1].remove(); document.querySelector('.hamburger_newsletter_container').style.display="block";
      ham_news_behavior();
    }
  }

})();
    </script>

                  </p>

Spark said that "we have stepped down from our position on the board and we are in the process of making arrangements to ensure we do not profit from our recent investment in Dispo."&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Dispo was &lt;a href="https://www.protocol.com/dispo-david-dobrik-photography-app" target="_blank"&gt;one of the hottest apps in social&lt;/a&gt;, valued at $200 million thanks to investments from VCs such as Spark and Alexis Ohanian's Seven Seven Six.&lt;/p&gt;

          <div class="widget tag-deepfakes post-section--china" data-category="Protocol | China" elid="2651145676">
           <article class="clearfix page-article sm-mb-1 quality-HD post-2651145676" data-is-frozen="false" elid="2651145676">
            <div class="row px10">
             <div class="col sm-mb-1" id="col-center" style="width:100.0%;">
              <div class="widget__body clearfix sm-mt-1">
               <h2 class="widget__headline h2">
                <a aria-label="Chinese deepfakes are going viral, and Beijing is freaking out" class="widget__headline-text custom-post-headline" data-type="text" href="https://www.protocol.com/china/chinese-deepfakes-regulators-alibaba-tencent">
                 Chinese deepfakes are going viral, and Beijing is freaking out
                </a>
               </h2>
               <div class="body js-expandable clearfix js-listicle-body css-listicle-body-2651145676">
                <div class="body-description">
                 <div class="widget__brief">
                  <p>
                   Beijing announced on Thursday that it has summoned eleven internet companies, including Alibaba, Tencent and ByteDance, over "audio-based social networking apps and apps that involve 'deepfake' technologies."
                  </p>
                 </div>
                 <div class="content-container">
                 </div>
                 <div class="js-appear-on-expand">
                  <template>
                   &lt;p&gt;The &lt;a href="http://www.cac.gov.cn/2021-03/18/c_1617648089558637.htm" target="_blank"&gt;announcement&lt;/a&gt; from China's Cyberspace Administration and Ministry of Public Security came as a direct response to an obsession among urban elites with Clubhouse-like apps and the rapid proliferation of viral DeepFakes in China. Protocol has covered the rise of the Clubhouse clones &lt;a href="https://www.protocol.com/bulletins/clubhouse-china-blowing-up-censorship" target="_self"&gt;here&lt;/a&gt;. But what's going on with DeepFakes? Here's what you should know:&lt;br&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul class="ee-ul"&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Thank Russia for China's deepfake craze. &lt;/strong&gt;At the end of February, Avatarify, an AI-based app developed by Russian engineers that transform static portrait photos into videos, trended on Douyin, the Chinese version of TikTok. Chinese users were quick to find innovative ways to create hilarious videos with the app, including one showing Elon Musk and Jack Ma seemingly singing the popular song &lt;a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=YnopHCL1Jk8" target="_blank"&gt;Dragostea Din Tei&lt;/a&gt; in sync. See for yourself&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;p class="shortcode-media shortcode-media-rebelmouse-image"&gt;
        &lt;img type="lazy-image" data-runner-src="https://www.protocol.com/media-library/eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpbWFnZSI6Imh0dHBzOi8vYXNzZXRzLnJibC5tcy8yNTg1MjkxNC9vcmlnaW4uZ2lmIiwiZXhwaXJlc19hdCI6MTY0OTU4NTIxNH0.20uUOV5vGGJijNyZNxFPOiOvGBd2j6MUNBy_TMTMZ2I/image.gif?width=980" id="73990" class="rm-shortcode" data-rm-shortcode-id="8f02c4ed670ad8ba921fda74a92c5b88" data-rm-shortcode-name="rebelmouse-image"&gt;
        &lt;small class="image-media media-caption" placeholder="Add Photo Caption..."&gt;Clocwise, from top left: Elon Musk, Mark Zuckerberg, Warren Buffet, Jack Ma, Wang Jianlin, Jia Yueting, Lei Jun, Pony Ma.&lt;/small&gt;&lt;small class="image-media media-photo-credit" placeholder="Add Photo Credit..."&gt;Protocol screengrab/Avatarify&lt;/small&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul class="ee-ul"&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;ul class="ee-ul"&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Deepfakes have gotten very popular in China very quickly. &lt;/strong&gt;Over 7 million Douyin users have used similar filters to create videos, and the videos have been watched over 2.7 billion times combined, according to&lt;a href="https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/lfKoyG3Ns24vZ7zB9xEpww" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank"&gt; the Chinese outlet TechSina&lt;/a&gt;. Taobao vendors started charging to create deepfakes, to people who don't have iPhones and thus can't use Avatarify themselves. On February 28, Avatarify topped the Chinese App Store chart; just two day later, it was pulled for reasons that were not made public.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;The videos that trended this time were mostly benign, &lt;/strong&gt;where ordinary users or even celebrities use their own photos for comedic effects. But AI face-swapping technologies have previously been used for creating pornographic content and disinformation. Academic researchers have been cautious in developing the commercial application of deepfake technologies, for this very matter. And no regulator wants to wait until there's a critical or incriminating deepfake of a Politburo member or Xi Jinping before taking action.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;The summons is essentially Beijing asking tech companies to conduct self-censorship &lt;/strong&gt;more quickly and thoroughly. The announcement cites &lt;a href="http://www.cac.gov.cn/2018-11/15/c_1123716072.htm" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank"&gt;a 2018 regulation&lt;/a&gt; that required Internet companies to conduct security assessments of their own apps and services when "online services that involve public opinionating or public organizing are introduced," or when "the number of users experiences a significant growth." &lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;China's now one of the world's deepfake capitals. &lt;/strong&gt;According to a &lt;a href="https://www.nisos.com/blog/deep-fakes/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank"&gt;deepfake white paper&lt;/a&gt; published by Nisos, a cybersecurity intelligence firm, Russia, Japan and China are the three most prominent countries where deepfake creators reside. In China, "the typical deep fake purveyor profile is more likely the hobbyist and researcher," the whitepaper says.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Chinese startups are trying to find a profit model for deepfake-like technologies.&lt;/strong&gt; Surreal, a one-year-old company backed by Sequoia and ZhenFund, said it wanted to become "the Google Translate of videos." It can modify people's facial characteristics and change the language they speak in videos, therefore reducing the cost of international marketing, the founder &lt;a href="https://www.36kr.com/p/1109621217175561" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank"&gt;told Chinese tech publication 36Kr&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;
                  </template>
                 </div>

Terms of the agreement were not disclosed. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;VMware is &lt;a href="https://www.protocol.com/enterprise/vmware-replacing-pat-gelsinger-dell" target="_blank"&gt;still looking for a permanent CEO&lt;/a&gt; to replace Patrick Gelsinger, who left for Intel earlier this year. &lt;/p&gt;

    <script>
     function isElementInViewport(el, extraOffsetTop, extraOffsetBottom) {
        var rectangle = el.getBoundingClientRect(),
            isHidden = rectangle.x === 0 && rectangle.y === 0 && rectangle.height === 0 && rectangle.top === 0;

        if (isHidden) {
            return false;
        }

        if (!extraOffsetTop) {
            extraOffsetTop = 0;
        }
        if (!extraOffsetBottom) {
            extraOffsetBottom = 0;
        }

        var extraTop = rectangle.top - extraOffsetTop,
            extraBottom = rectangle.bottom + extraOffsetBottom,
            windowHeight = document.documentElement.clientHeight,
            topVisible = extraTop > 0 && extraTop < windowHeight,
            bottomVisible = extraBottom < windowHeight && extraBottom > 0,
            overallVisible = extraTop < 0 && extraBottom > windowHeight;

        return topVisible || bottomVisible || overallVisible;
    }
  function Ithrottle (callback, limit) {
      var wait = false;
      return function () {
        if (!wait) {

          callback.apply(null, arguments);
          wait = true;
          setTimeout(function () {
            wait = false;
          }, limit);
        }
      }
    }
    </script>

function handleIntersection(entries) {
  entries.map((entry) => {
    if (entry.isIntersecting) {
      processAd(entry.target)
      observer.unobserve(entry.target);
    }
  });
}
function createElementChangeListener(selector, callback) {
    const initializedNodes = new Set([]);

    document.querySelectorAll(selector).forEach((node) => {
        callback(node);
        initializedNodes.add(node);
    });

    const mutationObserver = new MutationObserver(() => {
        const nodes = document.querySelectorAll(selector);
        nodes.forEach((node) => {
            if (!initializedNodes.has(node)) {
                callback(node);
                initializedNodes.add(node);
            }
        });
    });

    mutationObserver.observe(document.body, {
        childList: true,
        subtree: true,
    });
}
const observer = new IntersectionObserver(handleIntersection,options);
createElementChangeListener(".ad-place-holder",function(item){
observer.observe(item);
})
function processAd(ad_div) {
	googletag.cmd.push(function () {
		ad_id_count++;
		let ad_id = "homepage-waterfall-" + ad_id_count;
		ad_div.setAttribute("id", ad_id);
        ad_div.classList.add("proc");
        if(window.innerWidth > 767){
            if(ad_div.getAttribute('data-ad-size')=="bannerMapping"){
                googletag.defineSlot('/21901267728/Homepage', [   [728, 90],   [970, 90],   [970, 250]  ], ad_id).addService(googletag.pubads());
            }
            else{
                googletag.defineSlot('/21901267728/Homepage',   [300, 250], ad_id).addService(googletag.pubads());
            }
        }
        else{
            googletag.defineSlot('/21901267728/mobile',  [[320, 50],[300, 250],[300,50]], ad_id).defineSizeMapping(bannerMapping).addService(googletag.pubads()); 
        }
		googletag.display(ad_id);
	});
}
    

});

window.REBELMOUSE_LOW_TASKS_QUEUE.push(function(){

    
        function findFirstChildByClass(element, className) {
        var foundElement = null, found;
        function recurse(element, className, found) {
            for (var i = 0; i < element.childNodes.length && !found; i++) {
                var el = element.childNodes[i];
                var classes = el.className != undefined? el.className.split(" ") : [];
                for (var j = 0, jl = classes.length; j < jl; j++) {
                    if (classes[j] == className) {
                        found = true;
                        foundElement = element.childNodes[i];
                        break;
                    }
                }
                if(found)
                    break;
                recurse(element.childNodes[i], className, found);
            }
        }
        recurse(element, className, false);
        return foundElement;
    }

var breakingNews=document.querySelector(".breaking-news");

  }
}

window.REBELMOUSE_LOWEST_TASKS_QUEUE.push(function(){

    
        function onSectionClick(parent) {
    return function onClick() {
        parent
            .querySelector(".new-topbar-newsletter-mobile-submenu")
            .classList.toggle("new-topbar-mobile-submenu-active");
        var childNodes = parent.querySelector(
            ".new-topbar-newsletter-mobile-submenu"
        ).parentNode.parentNode.childNodes;
        for (var i = 0; i < childNodes.length; i++) {
            var subChildNodes = childNodes[i].childNodes;
            for (var j = 0; j < subChildNodes.length; j++) {
                if (
                    subChildNodes[j].classList.contains(
                        "new-topbar-more-mobile-submenu"
                    )
                ) {
                    subChildNodes[j].classList.remove(
                        "new-topbar-mobile-submenu-more-active"
                    );
                } else if (
                    !subChildNodes[j].classList.contains(
                        "new-topbar-newsletter-mobile-submenu"
                    )
                ) {
                    subChildNodes[j].classList.remove(
                        "new-topbar-mobile-submenu-active"
                    );
                }
            }
        }
    };
}

document
    .querySelectorAll(".new-topbar-newsletter-text-container")
    .forEach(function (el) {
        el.addEventListener(
            "click",
            onSectionClick(el.closest(".rebel-top-bar"))
        );
    });

    .querySelectorAll(".new-topbar-sections-text-container")

                        subChildNodes[j].classList.contains(
                            "new-topbar-more-mobile-submenu"
                        )
                    ) {
                        subChildNodes[j].classList.remove(
                            "new-topbar-mobile-submenu-more-active"
                        );
                    } else if (
                        !subChildNodes[j].classList.contains(
                            "new-topbar-sections-mobile-submenu"
                        )
                    ) {
                        subChildNodes[j].classList.remove(
                            "new-topbar-mobile-submenu-active"
                        );
                    }
                }
            }
        });
    });

document
    .querySelectorAll(".new-topbar-more-text-container")
    .forEach(function (el) {
        var parent = el.closest(".rebel-top-bar");
        el.addEventListener("click", function () {
            parent
                .querySelector(".new-topbar-more-mobile-submenu")
                .classList.toggle("new-topbar-mobile-submenu-more-active");

                ".new-topbar-more-mobile-submenu"

                for (var j = 0; j < subChildNodes.length; j++) {
                    if (

                            "new-topbar-more-mobile-submenu"
                        )
                    ) {

                    }

            }
        });
    });

document
    .querySelectorAll(".new-topbar-manuals-text-container")
    .forEach(function (el) {
        var parent = el.closest(".rebel-top-bar");
        el.addEventListener("click", function () {
            var dropdown = parent.querySelector("#manuals-dropdown-icon");
            if (dropdown.classList.contains("fa-chevron-down")) {
                dropdown.classList.add("fa-chevron-up");
                dropdown.classList.remove("fa-chevron-down");
            } else {
                dropdown.classList.add("fa-chevron-down");
                dropdown.classList.remove("fa-chevron-up");
            }
            parent
                .querySelector(".new-topbar-manuals-mobile-submenu")
                .classList.toggle("new-topbar-mobile-more-submenu-active");
        });
    });
    

});

window.REBELMOUSE_LOWEST_TASKS_QUEUE.push(function(){

    
        function setCookie(name,value,days) {var expires = "";if (days) {var date = new Date();date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days*24*60*60*1000));expires = "; expires=" + date.toUTCString();}document.cookie = name + "=" + (value || "") + expires + "; path=/";}

function getCookie(name) {var nameEQ = name + "=";var ca = document.cookie.split(';');for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {var c = ca[i];while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);}return null;}

function eraseCookie(name) {document.cookie = name +'=; Path=/; Expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT;';}

/*--------------------------*/

function resetR(a) {
  a.removeAttribute("class");
  a.innerHTML = "";
}

if(document.querySelector("#form_out").getAttribute('data-group')){
	let formGroup = document.querySelector("#form_out").getAttribute('data-group');
	var form_parts = formGroup.split("_");
}

var TS = ~~(+new Date() / 1000);

if (window.location.pathname != "/" && window.location.pathname != "/newsletters/" && window.location.pathname.split("/")[1] != "Sponsored-Content" && window.location.pathname.split("/")[1] != "manuals" && window.location.pathname != "/enterprise/about/" && window.location.pathname != "/china/about-protocol-china/" && window.location.pathname != "/join-source-code/"){
  
document.querySelectorAll("#form_wrap form").forEach(function (F) {
  F.addEventListener("submit", function (e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    if (F.querySelector("#robot").value !== "") {
      return false;
    }

    let groups = {};
    F.querySelectorAll("#groups input").forEach(function (I) {
      if (I.checked) {
        groups[I.getAttribute("name")] = true;
      }
    });
    
    var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
    xhr.open('POST', 'https://www.protocol.com/core/mail_lists/mailchimp/access/');
    xhr.setRequestHeader('Content-Type', 'application/json');
    xhr.onload = function() {
        if (xhr.status === 200) {
            var response = JSON.parse(xhr.responseText);
            let resp = F.querySelector("#resp");
            resetR(resp);

              if (response.created !== true) {
              resp.classList.add('bad');
              resp.innerHTML = 'Temporary error. Please try again later.';
            } else {
              resp.classList.add('good');
              email.value = '';
              resp.innerHTML = 'Thank you for subscribing!';
              
              if(form_parts[1]){
              	/* wait a week in random popup */
                if (getCookie("form_out_" + form_parts[1]) == null){
                  eraseCookie("form_out_" + form_parts[1]);
                  setCookie("form_out_" + form_parts[1],TS + 604800,8);
                }
              }
              
              /* set cookie that user subscribed and close in 3sec */
              if (getCookie("form_out_" + form_parts[0]) == null){
                eraseCookie("form_out_" + form_parts[0]);
                setCookie("form_out_" + form_parts[0],999999999999,9999);
                setTimeout(function () {
                 document.querySelector("#form_out").style.display = "none";
  				 document.querySelector("body").style.overflow = " visible";
                }, 3000);
              }
            }
        } else if (xhr.status === 400) {
            var response = JSON.parse(xhr.responseText);
            let resp = F.querySelector("#resp");
            resetR(resp);
            resp.innerHTML = response.error;
            resp.classList.add("bad");
        }
    };
    xhr.send(JSON.stringify({
        email: F.querySelector(".email").value,
        group_ids: groups,
        list_id: 'cd425f6479'
    }));
  });
});
}

function setpopupclose(forever) {
  document.querySelector("#form_out").style.display = "none";
  document.querySelector("body").style.overflow = " visible";
  
  if(forever){ 
  	var value = 999999999999; var days = 9999;
  }else{ 
  	var value = TS + 604800; var days= 8;
  }
  if(form_parts[1]){
  	if (getCookie("form_out_" + form_parts[1]) == null){
      eraseCookie("form_out_" + form_parts[1]);
      setCookie("form_out_" + form_parts[1], TS + 604800, 8);
    }
  }
  if(getCookie("form_out_" + form_parts[0]) == null){
      eraseCookie("form_out_" + form_parts[0]);
      setCookie("form_out_" + form_parts[0], value, days);
  }
}
document.querySelector("#form_out .cloz").onclick = function () {
  setpopupclose(0);
};
document.querySelector("#form_out .nottoday").onclick = function () {
  setpopupclose(1);
};

if (window.location.pathname != "/" && window.location.pathname != "/newsletters/" && window.location.pathname.split("/")[1] != "Sponsored-Content" && window.location.pathname.split("/")[1] != "manuals" && window.location.pathname != "/enterprise/about/" && window.location.pathname != "/china/about-protocol-china/"){
  
  var TS = ~~(+new Date() / 1000);
  let FO = parseInt(getCookie("form_out"));
  
  if(document.querySelector("#form_out").getAttribute('data-group')){
  
    if(form_parts[1]){
      if(!getCookie("form_out_" + form_parts[1])){
        if(!getCookie("form_out_" + form_parts[0]) || (!isNaN(FO) && FO < TS)) {
          setTimeout(function(){
            document.querySelector("#form_out").style.display = "inline-block";
            document.querySelector("body").style.overflow = " hidden";
          },2000)
        }
       }
    }else{
      if(!getCookie("form_out_" + form_parts[0]) || (!isNaN(FO) && FO < TS)) {
        setTimeout(function(){
          document.querySelector("#form_out").style.display = "inline-block";
          document.querySelector("body").style.overflow = " hidden";
        },2000)
      }
    }
    
  }
}
    

});

window.REBELMOUSE_LOWEST_TASKS_QUEUE.push(function(){

    
        var threshold=600;
REBELMOUSE_STDLIB.onElementInViewport({
  	selector: ".ad-place-holder:not(.processed)",
    isMatchingNode(node) {
        return node.classList.contains('ad-place-holder');
    },threshold,
    onIntersect(entry) {
      let ad_diiv=entry.target;
      console.log("iin view ad div onElementInViewport");
		googletag.cmd.push(function() {
           incontentMapping=  googletag.sizeMapping().
		addSize([768, 0], [[728, 90],[300, 250],[468, 60]]).
		addSize([0, 0], [[320, 50],[300, 250]]).
		build();
				
          ad_id_count++;
          let ad_id="site-ad-"+ad_id_count;
          
          ad_diiv.classList.add("processed")
          ad_diiv.setAttribute("id",ad_id);
          googletag.defineSlot(`/21901267728/${ad_modifier}`,  [[468, 60], [728, 90],  [300, 250]], ad_id).defineSizeMapping(incontentMapping).addService(googletag.pubads());
          googletag.display(ad_id); 
      	});
    }
});
    

});
